      var message = 'UncaughtException in ' + scriptSource + ' l:' + line + ' c:' + column + ' reason: ' +  msg;

          return true;
        }
        window.NREUM && window.NREUM.noticeError && window.NREUM.noticeError(scriptError, { msg: msg });
        return true;
      }

      throw err;
    };

      window.NREUM.setErrorHandler(function (err) {
        if (err.message === 'Script error.') return true;

                  var container = document.getElementById('search-results-mosaic-grid');
                  var styleEl = document.createElement('style');
                  var width = container.clientWidth - 1;
                  var rect;
                  function selectHeightBasedOnWidth(heights, width) {
  // Find the last height (iterate right to left)
  for (let i = heights.length - 1; i > 0; i -= 1) {
    const h = heights[i];

    if (width >= h.containerWidth) {
      return h.height;
    }
  }

  return (heights[0] || {
    height: 260
  }).height;
};
                  function pack(rectangles, rowWidth, targetRowHeight, {
  maxRows = null,
  usePercentageWidths = false,
  spacing = 0
} = {}) {
  let rowIndex = 1;
  let row = null;
  const tgtRowHeight = targetRowHeight - spacing;

  const newRow = () => ({
    width: 0,
    height: tgtRowHeight,
    aspect: 0,
    index: rowIndex,
    rectCount: 0
  }); // Step 1: Scale images to have height equal to targetRowHeight
  // and build up row objects. O(n) time and space.


  rectangles.forEach((rectangle, index) => {
    row = row || newRow();
    rectangle.height = tgtRowHeight;
    rectangle.width = calcWidth(rectangle.height, rectangle.aspect);
    const compareWidth = Math.min(rectangle.width, rowWidth);
    const remainingSpace = rowWidth - row.width; // Can't add the current rectangle to the current row; create a new row.

    if (row.width > 0 && remainingSpace < compareWidth * Math.min(1, tgtRowHeight / compareWidth)) {
      rowIndex += 1;
      row = newRow();
    }

    rectangle.row = row;
    row.width += rectangle.width;
    row.aspect = calcAspect(row.width, row.height);
    row.rectCount += 1;
    if (index === rectangles.length - 1) row.last = true;
  }); // Step 2: Scale images to their final size using the information
  // saved in the row objects. O(n) time, O(1) space. Skip last row if
  // the images would look too big if they were scaled up.

  for (let i = 0; i < rectangles.length; i += 1) {
    const rectangle = rectangles[i];
    const {
      row: currentRow
    } = rectangle;
    if (!maxRows) delete rectangle.row; // delete reference so row object can be garbage collected

    const finalRowWidth = rowWidth - spacing * currentRow.rectCount; // Normalize the current row if it's not the last row, OR
    // normalize the last row its contents take up at least 60 percent of the finalRowWidth

    if (!currentRow.last || currentRow.last && currentRow.width >= finalRowWidth * 0.6) {
      // Consider (micro) optimizing this step so it only happens when it needs to
      currentRow.width = finalRowWidth;
      currentRow.height = calcHeight(currentRow.width, currentRow.aspect);
    }

    rectangle.height = currentRow.height;
    rectangle.width = calcWidth(rectangle.height, rectangle.aspect);
    rectangle.rowIndex = currentRow.index;
    if (usePercentageWidths) rectangle.width = asPercentageOf(rectangle.width, finalRowWidth);
  }

  if (maxRows) {
    for (let i = rectangles.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
      if (rectangles[i].row.index === maxRows) {
        rectangles.splice(i + 1);
        return;
      }
    }
  }
};
                  var height = selectHeightBasedOnWidth(heights, width);
                  pack(
                    packed,
                    width,
                    height,
                    { usePercentageWidths: false, maxRows: null, spacing: 5 }
                  );
                  for (var i = 0; i < packed.length; i++) {
                    rect = packed[i];
                    styleStr += [
                      '#search-results-mosaic-grid .mosaic-grid-item-', i, ' {',
                      'width: ', rect.width, 'px !important;',
                      'height: ', rect.height, 'px !important;',
                      'margin: 2.5px !important;',
                      'padding: 0 !important;',
                      '}'
                    ].join('');
                  }
                  styleEl.innerText = styleStr;
                  container.appendChild(styleEl);
                  container.style.visibility = 'visible';
                }())
